***званый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:званый.html>зва́ный</a> (26475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ányj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:званый.html>зва́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zványj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>invited
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:званый.html>зва́ных</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>мало</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:избранный.html>и́збранных</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mnógo zványx, da malo ízbrannyx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">many are called, but few are chosen</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>with invited guests
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:званый.html>зва́ный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zványj</b> obéd</i> ― <span class="e-translation">formal dinner party; banquet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:званый.html>зва́ный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>ве́чер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zványj</b> véčer</i> ― <span class="e-translation">evening party; guest night</span></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>,  Mao Zedong,  <cite>Quotations from Chairman Mao Tse-tung</cite>, Classes and Class Struggle, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Quotations_from_Chairman_Mao_Tse-tung/Classes_and_Class_Struggle" class="extiw" title="s:Quotations from Chairman Mao Tse-tung/Classes and Class Struggle">chapter 2</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:революция.html>револю́ция</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:званый.html>зва́ный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́д</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Revoljúcija - éto ne <b>zványj</b> obéd</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A revolution is not a <b>dinner</b> party</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Short forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:званный.html>зван</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:званный.html>зва́на</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:званный.html>зва́но</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:званный.html>зва́ны</a></span> theoretically exist, but are usually avoided due to their similarity to short forms of the past passive participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

***звать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a> (545)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">зъвати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zŭvati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zъvati</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:позвать.html>позва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to call
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зову́т</a></b> Пётр.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Menjá <b>zovút</b> Pjótr.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">My name is Pyotr.</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">They <b>call</b> me Pyotr.</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to invite</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вызываться.html>вызыва́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vyzyvátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:призывать.html>призыва́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prizyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зваться.html>зва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be called</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>

***звезда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезда</a> (829)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gvězda</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zvezdá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезды́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звёзды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звёзд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">astronomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> star (celestial body)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:падающий.html>па́дающая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезда́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pádajuščaja <b>zvezdá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">shooting star</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезда́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:величина.html>величины́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zvezdá</b> pérvoj veličiný</i> ― <span class="e-translation">star of the first magnitude</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>star (celebrity)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезда́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:экран.html>экра́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zvezdá</b> ekrána</i> ― <span class="e-translation">movie star</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geometry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> star (geometric shape)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезда́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нарисованный.html>нарисо́ванная</a> им <a href = vnd.unilang:выделяться.html>выделя́лась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:среди.html>среди́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:остальной.html>остальны́х</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Zvezdá</b> narisóvannaja im vydeljálasʹ sredí ostalʹnýx.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The star drawn by him was outstanding among others.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mechanics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> spider</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:звездочка.html>звёздочка</a> (6038)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезда́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvezdá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-очка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-očka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gvězda</i> + diminutive suffix <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-очка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-očka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from diminutive infixes <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-к-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-k-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-к-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-k-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звездочка.html>звёздочка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zvjózdočka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звездочка.html>звёздочки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звездочка.html>звёздочки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звездочка.html>звёздочек</a></b>)

***звено.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:звено.html>звено́</a> (5480)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звено.html>звено́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zvenó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звено.html>звена́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звено.html>зве́нья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звено.html>зве́ньев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>link <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">element of a chain</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ключевой.html>ключево́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:звено.html>звено́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ključevóje <b>zvenó</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">crucial <b>link</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> part, branch; team, squad <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">smallest unit in a hierarchy or sequence</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2004</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>Сыны́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:север.html>Се́вера</a> (lyrics and music),  “Разочарование”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:орлиный.html>Орли́ный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взор.html>взор</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>Вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удаться.html>уда́стся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:погибнуть.html>поги́бнуть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бою́</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>Нет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слабый.html>сла́бых</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:звено.html>зве́ньев</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цепь.html>цепи́</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>Нет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слабый.html>сла́бых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воин.html>во́инов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>строю́</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vam ne udástsja pogíbnutʹ v bojú<br />Net slábyx <b>zvénʹjev</b> v cepí<br />Net slábyx vóinov v strojú</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You won’t succeed to die in battle<br />There are no weak <b>links</b> in the chain<br />No weak fighters in the line</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>

***звереть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:звереть.html>звере́ть</a> (20419)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зверь.html>зверь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zverʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звереть.html>звере́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zverétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озвереть.html>озвере́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fly into a rage</li>
<li>to become a beast, to become brutalized</li></ol>

***звериный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:звериный.html>звери́ный</a> (7347)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зверь.html>зверь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zverʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ínyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звериный.html>звери́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zverínyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>animal, feral</li>
<li>brutal, savage, wild, feral</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зверь.html>зверь</a> (1289)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zvěrь</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">θήρ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">thḗr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ferus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зверь.html>зверь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zverʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зверь.html>зве́ря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зверь.html>зве́ри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зверь.html>звере́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>animal, beast</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> brute</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sciences</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mammal</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зверюшка.html>зверю́шка</a> (25925)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зверь.html>зверь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zverʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ю́шка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-júška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зверюшка.html>зверю́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zverjúška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зверюшка.html>зверю́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зверюшка.html>зверю́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зверюшка.html>зверю́шек</a></b>)
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zvonъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звон.html>звон</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zvon</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звон.html>зво́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звон.html>зво́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звон.html>зво́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ring, jingle, chime <i>(sound)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вечерний.html>вече́рний</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:звон.html>звон</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">večérnij <b>zvon</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">evening bell</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:звонкий.html>зво́нкий</a> (4673)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звон.html>звон</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звонкий.html>зво́нкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zvónkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)зво́нче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sonorous, clear, soniferous</li>
<li>resonant</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">phonetics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> phonology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> voiced
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глухо́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gluxój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звонок.html>звоно́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zvonók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звонок.html>звонка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звонок.html>звонки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звонок.html>звонко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bell (signaling device such as a bicycle bell)</li>
<li>bell (an audible signal such as a school bell)</li>
<li>ring, call (a telephone call or telephone conversation)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звук.html>звук</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvuk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:звякать.html>звя́кать</a> (15415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">звꙗкати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvjakati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. </p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звякнуть.html>звя́кнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zvjáknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звякать.html>звя́кать</a></b>)

***здание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:здание.html>зда́ние</a> (993)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">зьдати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zĭdati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ание</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здание.html>зда́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zdánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здание.html>зда́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здание.html>зда́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здание.html>зда́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>building, edifice, structure</li></ol>
